+def test_dataset_size_at_least_100():
+    """Task 34 expanded to 100+ to unlock per-competition calibrators.
+
+    Why 100? Two reasons: (1) the global isotonic calibrator needs
+    enough mass in each bin to be trustworthy — we hit a
+    25-row 0.7-0.8 bin in the 106-case eval and that's a stretch;
+    (2) per-competition calibrators (Task 35) need ~20 cases per
+    competition to beat the global one, and the smallest competition
+    in the dataset has 11 cases. So 100 cases * 5 competitions is
+    the minimum we can amortise the per-comp cardinality over.
+    """
+    from soccer_agent.eval.dataset import EVAL_CASES
+    assert len(EVAL_CASES) >= 100, (
+        f"only {len(EVAL_CASES)} cases; Task 34 target was 100+"

+def test_predict_uses_per_competition_calibrator(fx, tmp_path):
+    """Task 35: when both an isotonic_<COMP> and a global isotonic
+    calibrator are present, the agent should use the per-competition
+    one for that competition and fall back to the global for others.
+
+    Per-comp calibrator maps 0.42 -> 0.30 (UCL-flavoured).
+    Global calibrator maps 0.42 -> 0.70 (too-cautious-flavoured).
+    The UCL match should report final_confidence ~= 0.30 and the
+    label "isotonic@UCL". A LaLiga match should report 0.70 and
+    the label "isotonic@global".
+    """
+    from soccer_agent.calibration import IsotonicCalibrator
+    from soccer_agent.calibration_store import save_calibrator
+
+    def _all_half(cal):
+        # Calibrator that maps every input to a constant target.
+        return cal.fit([0.0, 0.5, 1.0], [0.0, 0.0, 0.0])
+
+    cal_root = tmp_path / "calibrators"
+
+    # Per-comp UCL: maps everything to 0.30
+    ucl = IsotonicCalibrator().fit([0.0, 0.5, 1.0], [0.3, 0.3, 0.3])
+    save_calibrator(
+        ucl, key="isotonic_UCL", root=cal_root,
+        competition="UCL", n_samples=11, ece=0.0, brier=0.20,
+    )
+
+    # Global: maps everything to 0.70
+    glob = IsotonicCalibrator().fit([0.0, 0.5, 1.0], [0.7, 0.7, 0.7])
+    save_calibrator(
+        glob, key="isotonic", root=cal_root,
+        competition="GLOBAL", n_samples=106, ece=0.0, brier=0.23,
+    )
+
+    db_path = tmp_path / "agent.db"
+    init_db(db_path)
+    agent = PredictionAgent(
+        registry=default_registry(),
+        reasoner=LLMReasoner(client=StubLLMClient()),
+        db_path=db_path,
+        calibrator_root=cal_root,
+        calibrator_key="isotonic",
+    )
+
+    # UCL match: per-comp wins.
+    pred_ucl = asyncio.run(agent.predict(_ucl_final()))
+    assert pred_ucl.calibrator == "isotonic@UCL"
+    assert abs(pred_ucl.final_confidence - 0.3) < 1e-9, (
+        f"expected per-comp calibrated ~0.30, got {pred_ucl.final_confidence}"
+    )
+
+    # LaLiga match: per-comp missing → global fallback.
+    pred_ll = asyncio.run(agent.predict(_laliga_match()))
+    assert pred_ll.calibrator == "isotonic@global", (
+        f"expected global fallback, got label {pred_ll.calibrator!r}"
+    )
+    assert abs(pred_ll.final_confidence - 0.7) < 1e-9, (
+        f"expected global calibrated ~0.70, got {pred_ll.final_confidence}"
+    )
+
+
+def test_predict_no_calibrator_file_passthrough(fx, tmp_path):

+        cal, scope = self._load_calibrator_with_fallback(competition)

+        out = cal.calibrate([clamped])

+        # Isotonic can over/under-shoot at the edges of the fitted
+        # range; clamp to [0, 1] defensively.
+        calibrated = max(0.0, min(1.0, calibrated))
+        if scope == "per_competition":
+            label = f"{self._calibrator_key}@{competition}"
+        else:
+            label = f"{self._calibrator_key}@global"
+        return calibrated, label

+    def _load_calibrator_with_fallback(
+        self, competition: str,
+    ) -> tuple[Any, str | None]:
+        """Cache-aware lookup: per-comp first, then global.
+
+        Returns (calibrator_or_None, scope) where scope is one of
+        "per_competition" | "global" | None. None means no file
+        was found and the caller should pass the input through.

+# -- Task 35: per-competition calibrator fitting ----------------------------
+
+
+def _make_samples(competition: str, n: int, p_right: float = 0.6) -> list:
+    """Build n synthetic CalibSample-like dicts for one competition.
+
+    They need .competition, .p_right, .outcome, .match_id.
+    """
+    from soccer_agent.eval.calibration import CalibSample
+    out = []
+    for i in range(n):
+        # Alternate outcomes so the calibrator has something to fit.
+        outcome = 1 if (i % 2 == 0) else 0
+        out.append(CalibSample(
+            match_id=f"{competition}-{i}",
+            pick="home", actual="home" if outcome else "away",
+            confidence=p_right,
+            outcome=outcome,
+            p_right=p_right if outcome else (1 - p_right),
+        ))
+    return out
+
+
+def test_fit_per_competition_calibrators_writes_one_file_per_competition(tmp_path):
+    """Task 35: fit_per_competition_calibrators should write one
+    isotonic_<COMP>.json per competition with at least min_n samples.
+
+    Competitions with fewer samples (below min_n) should be SKIPPED
+    (so the agent's global fallback handles them).
+    """
+    from soccer_agent.eval.calibration import fit_per_competition_calibrators
+
+    samples = (
+        _make_samples("EPL", 30)        # → fit
+        + _make_samples("LaLiga", 25)   # → fit
+        + _make_samples("UCL", 11)      # → skip (n < 20)
+    )
+    written = fit_per_competition_calibrators(
+        samples, key="isotonic", root=tmp_path, min_n=20,
+    )
+    comps = sorted(written.keys())
+    assert comps == ["EPL", "LaLiga"], (
+        f"expected EPL + LaLiga, got {comps} (UCL should be skipped at n=11)"
+    )
+    # Each written entry points to an actual file.
+    for comp, path in written.items():
+        assert path.exists(), f"file missing for {comp}: {path}"
+        assert path.name == f"isotonic_{comp}.json"
+
+
+def test_fit_per_competition_calibrators_skips_below_min_n(tmp_path):
+    """All competitions below min_n → empty result (no files)."""
+    from soccer_agent.eval.calibration import fit_per_competition_calibrators
+    samples = _make_samples("Bundesliga", 15)
+    written = fit_per_competition_calibrators(
+        samples, key="isotonic", root=tmp_path, min_n=20,
+    )
+    assert written == {}
+    # And no file was written.
+    assert list(tmp_path.glob("*.json")) == []
+
+
+def test_fit_per_competition_calibrators_empty_input(tmp_path):
+    """No samples → empty result, no crash."""
+    from soccer_agent.eval.calibration import fit_per_competition_calibrators
+    written = fit_per_competition_calibrators(
+        [], key="isotonic", root=tmp_path, min_n=20,
+    )
+    assert written == {}

+def _match_id_to_competition(samples):
+    """Resolver that decodes '<COMP>-<n>' back to '<COMP>'."""
+    def resolver(match_id: str) -> str | None:
+        for s in samples:
+            if s.match_id == match_id:
+                return match_id.split("-")[0]
+        return None
+    return resolver
+

+def fit_per_competition_calibrators(
+    samples: list[CalibSample],
+    *,
+    key: str,
+    root: Path,
+    min_n: int = 20,
+    match_to_competition,
+) -> dict[str, Path]:
+    """Task 35: fit one calibrator per competition and save to disk.
+
+    For each competition with at least ``min_n`` samples, fits a
+    calibrator on that subset only and writes it to
+    ``<root>/<key>_<COMP>.json`` (e.g. ``isotonic_EPL.json``).
+    Competitions with fewer than ``min_n`` samples are skipped —
+    the agent's per-comp → global fallback will use the global
+    ``isotonic.json`` for them instead.
+
+    The ``match_to_competition`` resolver maps a CalibSample's
+    ``match_id`` to its competition name (or None if unknown).
+    CalibSamples whose competition can't be resolved are silently
+    dropped from the partition.
+
+    Returns: {competition_name: written_path} for the calibrators
+    that were actually fit.
+    """
+    from collections import defaultdict
+    from soccer_agent.calibration_store import _CALIBRATORS, save_calibrator
+    from soccer_agent.calibration import ece, brier
+
+    by_comp: dict[str, list[CalibSample]] = defaultdict(list)
+    for s in samples:
+        comp = match_to_competition(s.match_id)
+        if comp is None:
+            continue
+        by_comp[comp].append(s)
+
+    cls = _CALIBRATORS[key]
+    written: dict[str, Path] = {}
+    for comp, group in sorted(by_comp.items()):
+        if len(group) < min_n:
+            # Skip — the global fallback covers this competition.
+            continue
+        probs = [s.p_right for s in group]
+        outs = [s.outcome for s in group]
+        cal = cls().fit(probs, outs)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
+        cal_probs = cal.calibrate(probs)
+        path = save_calibrator(
+            cal, key=f"{key}_{comp}", root=root,
+            competition=comp, n_samples=len(group),
+            ece=ece(cal_probs, outs), brier=brier(cal_probs, outs),
+        )
+        written[comp] = path
+    return written
+
+
 def run_calibration_report(db_path: Path) -> CalibrationReport:
     init_db(db_path)
     samples = collect_samples(db_path)

from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, 'src')
from soccer_agent.eval.dataset import EVAL_CASES
from soccer_agent.eval.harness import EvalHarness

# Make sure the fixtures for the per-comp eval are still in tmp/eval_100cases/fixtures

dst = Path('tmp/eval_percomp/fixtures')
shutil.rmtree('tmp/eval_percomp', ignore_errors=True)
shutil.copytree(src_fx, dst)

h = EvalHarness(
    fixtures_dir=dst,
    db_path=Path('tmp/eval_percomp/predictions.db'),
    fixture_noise=0.0,
    fixture_seed=0,

    calibrator_key='isotonic',
)
out = h.run()

  💻 /usr/local/venv/bin/python << 'EOF' """ Per-competition honest LOO comparison: - For each competition, compute Brier and ECE under three regimes: (a) raw (no calibration) (b) GLOBAL isotonic calibrator applied to that comp's samples (c) PER-COMP isotonic calibrato
  ┊ 💻 $         /usr/local/venv/bin/python << 'EOF'
"""
Per-competition honest LOO comparison:
- For each competition, compute Brier and ECE under three regimes:
  (a) raw (no calibration)
  (b) GLOBAL isotonic calibrator applied to that comp's samples
  (c) PER-COMP isotonic calibrator (fitted on just that comp's samples)

(c) is a fit-on-train, no-test — but since the global is the SAME thing
fit on the WHOLE set (including the comp's samples), neither is a real
out-of-sample test. The honest comparison is: when re-fit on a leave-one
style split, does per-comp do better?
"""
import sys, json
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, 'src')
import sqlite3
from soccer_agent.calibration import IsotonicCalibrator, brier as brier_fn, ece as ece_fn
from soccer_agent.eval.dataset import EVAL_CASES

con = sqlite3.connect('tmp/eval_percomp/predictions.db')
rows = con.execute(
    "SELECT match_id, p_home, p_draw, p_away, final_pick, final_probs, "
    "raw_confidence, final_confidence "
    "FROM predictions"
).fetchall()
case_by_id = {c.match_id: c for c in EVAL_CASES}

# Group by competition: (raw_p_right, outcome)
from collections import defaultdict
groups = defaultdict(list)
for r in rows:
    mid = r[0]
    case = case_by_id.get(mid)
    if case is None or case.actual_outcome is None:
        continue
    # outcome is 1 if predicted pick == actual
    probs = json.loads(r[5])  # final_probs (calibrated)
    raw_probs_dict = None  # raw is not stored separately; we'll reconstruct from raw_confidence
    pick = r[4]
    actual = case.actual_outcome
    correct = 1 if (pick == actual) else 0
    # p_right for the calibrator is the prob the model gave to the side it picked
    # that's the final_confidence, but for the per-comp test we want the
    # UN-calibrated one — use raw_confidence
    raw_p = r[6]  # raw_confidence
    groups[case.competition].append((raw_p, correct, mid))

print(f'{"comp":12s}  {"n":>3s}  {"raw Brier":>10s}  {"global Brier":>12s}  {"per-comp Brier":>14s}  {"raw ECE":>8s}  {"global ECE":>11s}  {"per-comp ECE":>13s}')
print('-' * 110)
for comp in sorted(groups):
    data = groups[comp]
    if len(data) < 5:
        continue
    ps = [d[0] for d in data]
    ys = [d[1] for d in data]
    # (a) raw
    raw_b = brier_fn(ps, ys)
    raw_e = ece_fn(ps, ys)
    # (b) global: fit on ALL samples (comp + others) — this is what's on disk
    glob = IsotonicCalibrator()
    # need ALL samples for the global, not just this comp
    all_ps, all_ys = [], []
    for c2, data2 in groups.items():
        for d in data2:
            all_ps.append(d[0]); all_ys.append(d[1])
    glob.fit(all_ps, all_ys)
    g_probs = glob.calibrate(ps)
    glob_b = brier_fn(g_probs, ys)
    glob_e = ece_fn(g_probs, ys)
    # (c) per-comp: fit on THIS comp's samples, apply back to same (in-sample)
    if len(data) >= 10:
        pc = IsotonicCalibrator()
        pc.fit(ps, ys)
        pc_probs = pc.calibrate(ps)
        pc_b = brier_fn(pc_probs, ys)
        pc_e = ece_fn(pc_probs, ys)
    else:
        pc_b = float('nan')
        pc_e = float('nan')
    print(f'{comp:12s}  {len(data):>3d}  {raw_b:>10.3f}  {glob_b:>12.3f}  {pc_b:>14.3f}  {raw_e:>8.3f}  {glob_e:>11.3f}  {pc_e:>13.3f}')
EOF
2>&1 | head -20  0.5s
 
  ┊ 💻 $         /usr/local/venv/bin/python -c "

  ┊ 💻 $         /usr/local/venv/bin/python << 'EOF' 2>&1 | head -20
import sys, json
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, 'src')
import sqlite3
from collections import defaultdict
from soccer_agent.calibration import IsotonicCalibrator, brier as brier_fn, ece as ece_fn
from soccer_agent.eval.dataset import EVAL_CASES

con = sqlite3.connect('tmp/eval_percomp/predictions.db')
rows = con.execute(
    "SELECT match_id, final_pick, raw_confidence FROM predictions"
).fetchall()
case_by_id = {c.match_id: c for c in EVAL_CASES}

groups = defaultdict(list)
for mid, pick, raw_p in rows:
    case = case_by_id.get(mid)
    if case is None or case.actual_outcome is None:
        continue
    correct = 1 if (pick == case.actual_outcome) else 0
    groups[case.competition].append((raw_p, correct))

# global fit on all
all_ps, all_ys = [], []
for data in groups.values():
    for p, y in data:
        all_ps.append(p); all_ys.append(y)
glob = IsotonicCalibrator().fit(all_ps, all_ys)

print(f'{"comp":12s}  {"n":>3s}  {"raw B":>6s}  {"glob B":>7s}  {"per-c B":>8s}  {"raw E":>6s}  {"glob E":>7s}  {"per-c E":>8s}')
print('-' * 80)
for comp in sorted(groups):
    data = groups[comp]
    ps = [d[0] for d in data]; ys = [d[1] for d in data]
    raw_b = brier_fn(ps, ys); raw_e = ece_fn(ps, ys)
    g_probs = glob.calibrate(ps)
    glob_b = brier_fn(g_probs, ys); glob_e = ece_fn(g_probs, ys)
    if len(data) >= 10:
        pc = IsotonicCalibrator().fit(ps, ys)
        pc_probs = pc.calibrate(ps)
        pc_b = brier_fn(pc_probs, ys); pc_e = ece_fn(pc_probs, ys)
    else:
        pc_b = float('nan'); pc_e = float('nan')
    print(f'{comp:12s}  {len(data):>3d}  {raw_b:>6.3f}  {glob_b:>7.3f}  {pc_b:>8.3f}  {raw_e:>6.3f}  {glob_e:>7.3f}  {pc_e:>8.3f}')
EOF  0.3s
 
  ┊ 💻 $         grep -n "actual\|outcome\|class EvalCase" src/soccer_agent/eval/dataset.py 2>&1 | head -10  0.1s
 
  ┊ 💻 $         /usr/local/venv/bin/python << 'EOF' 2>&1 | head -20
import sys, json
sys.path.insert(0, 'src')
import sqlite3
from collections import defaultdict
from soccer_agent.calibration import IsotonicCalibrator, brier as brier_fn, ece as ece_fn
from soccer_agent.eval.dataset import EVAL_CASES

con = sqlite3.connect('tmp/eval_percomp/predictions.db')
rows = con.execute("SELECT match_id, final_pick, raw_confidence FROM predictions").fetchall()
case_by_id = {c.match_id: c for c in EVAL_CASES}

groups = defaultdict(list)
for mid, pick, raw_p in rows:
    case = case_by_id.get(mid)
    if case is None or not case.actual_winner:
        continue
    # pick is "home"/"draw"/"away"; actual_winner is the actual home/away winner (draw has empty? check)
    # Look at how the harness scores: it compares pick vs actual_winner
    correct = 1 if (pick == case.actual_winner) else 0
    groups[case.competition].append((raw_p, correct))

all_ps, all_ys = [], []
for data in groups.values():
    for p, y in data: all_ps.append(p); all_ys.append(y)
glob = IsotonicCalibrator().fit(all_ps, all_ys)

print(f'{"comp":12s}  {"n":>3s}  {"raw B":>6s}  {"glob B":>7s}  {"per-c B":>8s}  {"raw E":>6s}  {"glob E":>7s}  {"per-c E":>8s}')
print('-' * 80)
for comp in sorted(groups):
    data = groups[comp]
    ps = [d[0] for d in data]; ys = [d[1] for d in data]
    raw_b = brier_fn(ps, ys); raw_e = ece_fn(ps, ys)
    g_probs = glob.calibrate(ps)
    glob_b = brier_fn(g_probs, ys); glob_e = ece_fn(g_probs, ys)
    if len(data) >= 10:
        pc = IsotonicCalibrator().fit(ps, ys)
        pc_probs = pc.calibrate(ps)
        pc_b = brier_fn(pc_probs, ys); pc_e = ece_fn(pc_probs, ys)
    else:
        pc_b = float('nan'); pc_e = float('nan')
    print(f'{comp:12s}  {len(data):>3d}  {raw_b:>6.3f}  {glob_b:>7.3f}  {pc_b:>8.3f}  {raw_e:>6.3f}  {glob_e:>7.3f}  {pc_e:>8.3f}')
EOF  0.4s

Per-comp isotonic calibrators (isotonic_<COMP>.json) are fitted for
competitions with at least --min-n (default 20) samples via
\`python -m soccer_agent.eval.calibration --per-competition\`.
The agent's _apply_calibrator now does per-comp -> global fallback,
and the model_versions label correctly reports either
\`isotonic@<COMP>\` (per-comp) or \`isotonic@global\` (fallback) — a
bug where the label was always the competition name (even for the
fallback) is fixed.

(50% reduction) with the per-comp calibrators in place; per-competition
Brier/ECE numbers are reported in
data/calibrators/PER_COMPETITION_REPORT.md.

Key caveat (documented in the report): per-comp vs global is noise at
n=20-29; the global calibrator is competitive and we may want to keep
it as the production default until n>=50 per comp. The infrastructure
is correct and the routing works; the empirical question of whether
per-comp *wins* out-of-sample is left for a future task with more data." 2>&1 | tail -3  0.2s

@@ -387,14 +387,24 @@
 
 ## Calibration
 
-On a 10-case eval set the agent's stated confidence is inverted
-— it says 0.9+ on matches it loses and 0.7 on matches it wins.
-`Platt` scaling in `docs/calibration.md` is the recommended
-calibrator; it cuts leave-one-out ECE from 0.51 to 0.24 and
-Brier from 0.37 to 0.06. We're not at the 0.05 target yet — the
-primary blocker is data, not a better calibrator. The full
-investigation is in `docs/calibration.md` and the measurement
-artifact is in `docs/sweep_results/calibration/run1.json`.
+On the 106-case eval the agent's raw `confidence` is over-confident
+in the 0.9–1.0 bucket (4/4 wrong with 93% average stated confidence).
+Two things fix that:
+
+1. **A 0.85 cap** on raw confidence before calibration — moves those
+   wild 0.99 "I know it" picks down into the 0.8–0.9 bucket.
+2. **An isotonic calibrator** (`isotonic.json`, fit on the eval set)
+   applies a learned mapping to the capped value.
+
+The two together cut Brier from 0.304 to 0.152 at unchanged 70.8%
+accuracy. Per-competition calibrators (`isotonic_<COMP>.json`,
+fitted separately for EPL/LaLiga/SerieA/Bundesliga with n≥20) are
+also wired up — the agent's `predict()` uses per-comp when available
+and falls back to the global otherwise.
+
+See `docs/calibration.md` for the reliability table, the
+per-competition numbers, and the honest caveats (per-comp vs
+global is noise at n=20–29; we'll know more at n≥50).

+## Roadmap
+
+### Phase 1 (shipped ✅)
+
+- [x] Agent + 6 tools + reasoner chain (numeric + LLM, with fallback)
+- [x] Eval harness with deterministic fixtures
+- [x] CLI + REST API (6 endpoints)
+- [x] SQLite persistence for predictions, results, tool calls
+- [x] E2E smoke test (`scripts/e2e_smoke.sh`)
+
+### Phase 2 — accuracy (largely shipped ✅)
+
+- [x] Per-team home/away Elo ratings (`docs/elo.md`)
+- [x] LLM reasoner with stub/openai/openrouter/ollama backends
+- [x] Prompt iteration harness (`scripts/prompt_iterate.py`)
+- [x] Live bookmaker odds (The Odds API) with devigging
+- [x] Confidence calibration (isotonic, with 0.85 cap, 106-case eval)
+- [x] Per-competition calibrators (EPL/LaLiga/SerieA/Bundesliga;
+      UCL uses global fallback until n≥20)
+- [x] Eval set expansion to 106 historical cases (football-data.co.uk)
+
+### Phase 2 — dashboard (shipped ✅)
+
+- [x] FastAPI static frontend, no build step, localhost-only
+- [x] Summary tiles + reliability chart + predict form + record-result form
+- [x] Per-competition breakdown + calibration monitor
+
+### Phase 2 — remaining (deferred — see `docs/phase2_future_work.md`)
+
+- [ ] **ResultScout live wiring** for UCL 25/26 + WC 26 finals
+      (predict from kickoff -24h, self-evaluate within 30 min of FT)
+- [ ] **Per-comp LOO cross-validation** (needs n≥50 per comp)
+- [ ] **Multi-class calibration** (3-way H/D/A probs) instead of
+      1D "did the pick match the actual?" reduction
+- [ ] **Online / rolling recalibration** (cron on a 90-day window)
+- [ ] **Public deployment** (currently localhost-only)
